  && a + A == b + B

      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {

    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {

      }

    return false;

      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)

        assert tot == 3 * des;
        assert a + A == des;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n by {
    assert 3 * des == tot;
  }

  return true;

    assert (des + des + des) - (a + b + c) == 3 * des - (a + b + c);
    assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n;
  }

  return true;

  exists A: int, B: int, C: int
    :: ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
}

method CollectingCoins(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int) returns (result: bool)
  requires a >= 0 && b >= 0 && c >= 0 && n >= 0
  ensures result == CanDistribute(a, b, c, n)
{
  var tot := a + b + c + n;
  if tot % 3 != 0 {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  var des := tot / 3;
  if a > des || b > des || c > des {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
        assert tot == 3 * des;
        assert a + A == des;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n;
  assert des >= a && des >= b && des >= c;
  assert 3 * des == tot;
  assert 3 * (des - a) == tot - 3 * a;
  assert tot - 3 * a == tot - 3 * a;
  assert tot == a + b + c + n;
  assert 3 * des == a + b + c + n;
  assert des == (a + b + c + n) / 3;
  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n;
  assert des >= a;
  assert des >= b;
  assert des >= c;
  return true;
}

{
  A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0
  && A + B + C == n
  && a + A == b + B
  && a + A == c + C
}

ghost predicate CanDistribute(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int)
  requires n >= 0
{
  exists A: int, B: int, C: int
    :: ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
}

method CollectingCoins(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int) returns (result: bool)
  requires a >= 0 && b >= 0 && c >= 0 && n >= 0
  ensures result == CanDistribute(a, b, c, n)
{
  var tot := a + b + c + n;
  if tot % 3 != 0 {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  var des := tot / 3;
  if a > des || b > des || c > des {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
        assert tot == 3 * des;
        assert a + A == des;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n;
  // the above follows from: 3*des == tot and tot = a+b+c+n
  // so 3*des = a+b+c+n => des = (a+b+c+n)/3, hence des - a + des - b + des - c = n
  return true;
}

ghost predicate ValidDistribution(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int, A: int, B: int, C: int)
{
  A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0
  && A + B + C == n
  && a + A == b + B
  && a + A == c + C
}

ghost predicate CanDistribute(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int)
  requires n >= 0
{
  exists A: int, B: int, C: int
    :: ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
}

method CollectingCoins(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int) returns (result: bool)
  requires a >= 0 && b >= 0 && c >= 0 && n >= 0
  ensures result == CanDistribute(a, b, c, n)
{
  var tot := a + b + c + n;
  if tot % 3 != 0 {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
        assert 3 * (a + A) != tot; // Contradiction: tot % 3 != 0
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  var des := tot / 3;
  if a > des || b > des || c > des {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
        assert tot == 3 * des;
        assert a + A == des;
        assert a > des; // Contradiction
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n by {
    assert 3 * des == tot;
    assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == 3 * des - (a + b + c);
    assert 3 * des - (a + b + c) == tot - (a + b + c);
    assert tot == a + b + c + n;
    assert tot - (a + b + c) == n;
  }

  return true;
}
